 america kii arthvyavastha main jaan daalane ke liye vahaan kii fedral reserve ne dollar kii maatra badha di or kah diya ki ab federell reserve band nahin kharidega
 This had an impact on markets and currencies around the world
 isi ko temper tentaram kehete hai
 When ever the price of crude oil increases in the world market, then the currency starts to weaken
 is baar turki ke kaaran ye giravat ai he
 Politics has to be chosen only when it has to leave these arguments and run its own shop
 jhooth bolnaa hota he
 You know that at the moment there is a trade war between the US and China
 aae din donon mulk ek duusare ke aayaat par tex badha dete hai
 At this time, America's economy is in a strong position, due to this, the flow of dollars is going towards America
 america niveshak duusare bazaaron se paisa nikaalkar apane market main laga rahe hai
 Taking advantage of this strength, Trump has opened a front against China
 china bhi america se aaayaatit chizon par aayaat shulk badhaate ja rahaa he
 This is having an impact on other countries as well
 america ek saath china, iran, turki, bharat sahit kai deshon ke khilaaf bhida hua he
 India has also increased import duties on many American items
 ek angel america or turki aapas main bhide hue hai
 The US has increased the import duty of steel and aluminum from Turkey from 20 percent to 50 percent
 isse hoga yah ki turki ke steel kii maang kam ho jaaegi
 Angry with this, Turkish President Erdogan has said that his country will boycott American electronics
 unke stand ko dekhakar kayaas lagaae ja rahe hai ki kya vaaki aisa karenge yaa sirf dhamkee ke level par kaha he
 Erdogan has said that we will make better in our country than what we ask from America
 agar unke paas ai phone he to samsung bhi he
 There is Venus in our country
 ye sabhi phone ke brands hai
 It is not yet clear whether Ergodan will formalize it or the matter is limited to intimidation
 is vyapaarik jang main turki lira pichley maheene 25 fisadi kamazor ho gaya
 The comments 2016 main sibar haikaron ne bangladesh ke central bank ko hack kar liya or 101 milayan dollar nikaal liye
 Of this, 20 million dollars went to Sri Lankan hackers, which was recovered
 81 million dollar philipinos chalaa gaya tha jisamen se 18 million dollar waapas mil gaya tha
 There is no further information, but i am telling you that this kind of effort has been made in India too
 pune ke ek coparative bank se haikaron ne 94 karod uda liye hai
 Our colleague Sunil Singh has sent a report that money has been withdrawn through debit cards in 29 countries including India
 bharat main isse pehle itani badi sibar dakaiti nahin hui thi
 On August 11, the bank's switching system was hacked, and 12,000 transactions were carried out in 28 countries within 7 hours and 78 crore were withdrawn
 bharat ke bheetar 2849 baar tranjection hua or dhai karod nikaal liye gaye
 Then on August 13, 14 crore more were flown
 kaasmaas bank ne do dinon ke liye apana pement system band kar diya he magar graahakon ko dilasa diya he ki unka paisa surakshit he
 Do not worry
 bank ne epa ai aar darj kara diya he
 Does the government have a role in weakening the rupee? No
 phir yahi baat sarkaar khud se kyon nahin kahati he
 Only the government can answer this, but you can guess why the government does not say that the rupee has not weakened because of it
 kyonki jaise hi vah yah baat kahegi log puuchhenge ki phir vah kaise kaha karti thi ki rupaya upie sarkaar kii nitiyon ke kaaran kamazor ho rahaa tha
 We have asked Pranjay Guha Thakurta if he can explain the reasons which caused the rupee to weaken
 sarkaar kaa role nahin hota he
 Belongs to the Reserve Bank of India
 wo chaahe to dollar bech kar bazaar main isaki supplai badha de or rupee ko girane se roak le
 Due to the weakening of the rupee against the dollar, the most impact is on the price of petrol diesel
 petrol ke daam badhane lagate hai
 Also, the import of goods from outside starts to be expensive
 rupaya kamazor hoga to videshi niveshak ko ritern kam milegaa
 However, the government has opted out of rupee politics
 vipaksh ne use gale laga liya he
 By the way, what BJP spokesperson Nalin Kohli has said is a matter of work
 unhone kaha he ki jo log akhbaar padhate hai unhen pataa he ki kyon ho rahaa he ye sab
 India's Economic Affairs Secretary Subhash Chander Garg has told Reuters that there is no need to worry about this because this fall in rupee is coming due to external factor
 duusari arthvyavasthaaon kii karency bhi kamazor ho rahi he
 At this stage, the Reserve Bank's attempt to curb the fall by selling dollars will not be of much benefit
 agar rupaya gir kar 80 par bhi aa jaae to bhi yah chintaa kii baat nahin hogi
 The second currency also kept getting weaker
 kahaan wo bharat tha jahaan 68 rupee ho jane par desh kaa swaabhaamin khatre main tha, aaj aarthik maamalon ke sachiv kehete hai ki ek dollar 80 rupee kaa bhi ho jayega to bhi chintaa kii baat nahin bas anya deshon kii karency kaa bhav bhi kamazor hota rahe
 Either the logic has changed or indeed the world has changed
 to kya 80 rupaya ho jayega
 Was the Indian Rupee falling only before 2013, the currency of other countries was not falling
 bilkul us vakt bhi yahi ho rahaa tha
 According to an article in Live Mint, Turkish lira has recorded the biggest fall apart from Indian rupee at this time
 is saal lira kaa mulya 45 pratishat kam ho gaya he
 For this reason, the euro has also weakened against the dollar
 newzealand kaa dollar bhi do saal main sabase adhik tutaa he
 The South African dollar has also fallen by 8 percent
 argentina kaa peso itnaa gira ki bainkon ne 5 pratishat byaaz daren badha di hai
 Does India's rupee also weaken when the currencies of other countries are weak
 kya aisa koi sambandh he
 Even in 2013, when the Indian rupee was weakening, the Turkish lira was also weakening
 iskaa matlab yah nahin ki donon kaa aapas main koi sambandh he
 There are many other reasons in between
 anya deshon kii mudraon kaa asar padataa he lekin kai baar bhartiya rupaya tab bhi kamazor hota he jab anya deshon kii mudraaen majboot ho rahi hoti hai
 Was watching a December 17, 2014 article on Live Mint
 tab bhartiya rupaya 13 maheene ke sabase nunatam str par tha
 Against the dollar
 us vakt dakshin korea kii karency won majboot ho rahi thi
 Japana's Yen also 1
 17 pratishat bhi majboot hua tha
 Singapore dollar, Malaysia's ringette was also strengthened

 bhartiya reserve bank kaa hota he
 If he wants to sell the dollar, increase its supply in the market and stop the rupee from falling
 dollar ke mukaable rupaya kamazor hone se sabase adhik asar petrol deazal ke daam par padataa he
 Petrol prices start rising
 saath hi baahar se chizon kaa aayaat mahangaa hone lagata he
 If the rupee is weak then the foreign investor will get less returns
 baharhaal rupee kii raajnneeti se sarkaar ne kinaaraa kar liya he
 The opposition has embraced him
 vaise bijepi ke pravaktaa nalin kohli ne jo kaha he wo kaam kii baat kahi he
 He has said that those who read newspapers know why all this is happening
 bharat ke aarthik maamalon ke sachiv subhash chander garg ne riter se kaha he ki ise lekar chintaa karne kii koi zarurat nahin he kyoki rupee main yah giravat bahari factor ke kaaran aa rahi he
 The currency of other economies is also weakening
 is str par reserve bank ke dollar bech kar giravat ko rokane kii koshish kaa khaas phayda nahin hoga
 Even if the rupee falls to 80, it will not be a matter of concern
 barshate duusari karency bhi kamazor hoti rahi
 Where was the India where the country's independence was in danger when it became 68 rupees, today the Secretary of Economic Affairs says that even a dollar will be 80 rupees, even if there is no worry, the currency of other countries will also be weak 
 yaa to tark badal gaya he yaa vaaki zamana badal gaya he
 So will it be 80 rupees? kya 2013 ke pehle sirf bhartiya rupaya gir rahaa tha, anya deshon kii karency main giravat nahin aa rahi thi
 Exactly the same was happening at that time
 live mint ke ek lekh ke anusaar is vakt bhartiya rupee ke alaava turki ke lira main sabase adhik giravat darj hui he
 The value of the lira has dropped 45 percent this year
 is kaaran euro kaa bhav bhi dollar ke mukaable kamazor hue he
 The New Zealand dollar is also the most broken in two years
 dakshin africa dollar kaa bhav bhi 8 pratishat gir gaya he
 The peso in Argentina fell so much that banks have increased interest rates by 5 percent
 kya jab anya deshon kii mudraaen kamazor hoti hai to bharat kaa rupaya bhi kamazor hota he
 Is there any such relationship? 2013 main bhi jab bhartiya rupaya kamazor ho rahaa tha tab turki kaa lira bhi kamazor ho rahaa tha
 This does not mean that the two have any relationship
 bich main bhi kai anya kaaran hote hai
 The currencies of other countries have an impact but sometimes the Indian rupee is weak even when the currencies of other countries are getting stronger
 live mint par 17 disambar 2014 kaa ek lekh dekh rahaa tha
 The Indian rupee was then at a 13-month low
 dollar ke mukaable
 At that time, South Korea's currency won were getting stronger
 japaana kaa yen bhi 1
 17 percent was also strengthened
 singapore kaa dollar, malaysia kaa ringet bhi majboot hua tha
 The currency crisis was disintegrating due to the crisis of the European Union in 2011 and the financial crisis in Greece in 2012 affected the currencies of the world
 28 agast 2013 ko jab bharat kaa rupaya ek dollar ke mukaable 68 par pahunchaa tha tab ek pramukh kaaran temper tentaram bhi tha
 To reinvigorate the US economy, the Federal Reserve increased the dollar and said that the Fed would no longer buy the Reserve Bond
 iskaa asar duniya bhar kii bazaaron or karency par padaa tha
 This is called the taper tantrum
 kabhi duniya ke bazaar main kachche tel kaa daam badhata he to karency kamazor hone lagati he
 This time it has declined due to turkey
 bas raajnneeti ko chunanaa hota he ki use kab in tarkon ko kinare kar apni dukaan chalaani hoti he
 Lies have to be told
 aap jaanate hai ki is vakt america or china ke bich vyapaarik yuddh chal rahaa he
 Both countries increase taxes on each other's imports
 is vakt america kii arthvyavastha majboot sthiti main he is kaaran bhi duniya bhar dollar kaa pravaah america kii taraf ho rahaa he
 American investors are withdrawing money from other markets and investing in their markets
 is majbooti kaa laabh uthaakar trump ne china ke khilaaf morcha khol diya he
 China is also increasing the import duty on goods imported from America
 iskaa asar duusare mulkon par bhi pad rahaa he
 The United States has clashed against many countries including China, Iran, Turkey, India simultaneously
 bharat ne bhi kai amareeki chizon par aayaat shulk badha diya he
 An Angle America and Turkey are at loggerheads
 america ne turki se steel or alumunium kaa aayaat shulk 20 pratishat se badhaakar 50 pratishat kar diya he
 This will reduce the demand for turkey steel
 isse gussa hokar turki ke raashtrapati erdogan ne kaha he ki unka desh amareeki electronics kaa bahishkaar karegaa
 Looking at their stand, speculations are being made as to whether they will really do this or just say at the level of threat
 erdogan ne kaha he ki ham jo bhi america se mangate hai usase behatar apane desh main bana lenge
 If they have an iphone, then so is Samsung
 hamaare desh main venus he
 These are all brands of phones
 yah abhi saaf nahi he ki argodan ise aupchaarik rup denge yaa abhi maamla dhamkee tak hi simit he
 The turkey lira weakened 25 percent in this trade war last month
 tippaniyan In 2016 cyber hackers hacked the Central Bank of Bangladesh and pulled out $ 101 million
 isamen se 20 milayan dollar srilanka ke haikaron ke paas gaya tha, jise waapas hasil kar liya gaya
 $ 81 million was gone to the Philippines, of which $ 18 million was returned
 iske aage kii jaankaree nahin he magar ye isliye bataa rahaa hum ki bharat main bhi is tarah kaa prayaas hua he
 The hackers have flown 94 crores from a co-operative bank in Pune
 hamaare sahyogi sunil singh ne report bheji he ki bharat sahit 29 deshon main debit card ke zarie paise nikaale gaye hai
 Never before has there been such a huge cyber robbery in India
 11 agast ko bank ke sweaching system ko hack kar 7 ghante ke bheetar 28 deshon main 12 hazaar baar tranjection hua or 78 karod nikaal liye gaye
 There were 2849 transactions within India and two and a half crores were withdrawn
 phir 13 agast ko 14 karod or uda liye
 Kasamas Bank has shut down its payment system for two days but has comforted customers that their money is safe
 chintaa na karen
 The bank has registered an FIR

 1757 AD kii plasi kii ladaai or 1764 i
 After the British won the battle of Buxar, the British East India Company tightened its hold on Bengal
 isi shashan ko apane anukool banaae rakhane ke liye angrejon ne samay-samay par kai act paarit kiye, jo bhartiya samvidhan ke vikaas kii seedhiyaan baniin
 They are: 1
 1773 i
 Regulating Act of: Under this Act, a Government was established in the Calcutta Presidency, consisting of the Governor General and four members of his Council, who used their power jointly
 isaki mukhya baaten is prakaar hai -(i)company ke shashan par sansadeey niyantran sthapit kiya gaya
 (ii) The Governor of Bengal was appointed the General of the three Presidencies
 (iii)kalakatta main ek supreme court kii sthapana kii gai
 2
 1784 i
 Ka Pitt's India Act: This Act introduced dual administration - (i) Court of Directors - for business affairs (ii) Board of Controllers - for political affairs
 3
 1793 A
D
 kaa charter adhinium:iske dwaara niyantran board ke sadasyon tathaa karmchaariyon ke vetan aadi ko bhartiya rajasav main se dene kii vyavastha kii gai
 4
 1813 i
 Charter Act of: (i) The Charter of the Company was extended for 20 years
 (ii)company ke bharat ke saath vyaper karne ke ekadhikaar ko chin liya gaya
 But it had a monopoly for 20 years regarding trade with China and trade in tea with eastern countries
 (iii)kuch simaaon ke adheen sabhi british nagarikon ke liye bharat ke saath vyapaar khol diya gaya
 5
 1833 i
 Charter Act of: Hereby (i) the business rights of the company were completely abolished
 (ii)ab company kaa kaary british sarkaar kii ore se maatr bharat kaa shashan karnaa rah gaya
 (iii) The Governor of Bengal was called the Governor General of India
 (iv)bhartiya kanoonon kaa vargeekaran kiya gaya tathaa is kaary ke liye vidhi ayog kii niyukti kii vyavastha kii gai
 6
 1853 i
 Charter Act of: By this Act, the principle of nomination in services was abolished and arrangements were made to fill important posts of the company on the basis of competitive examinations
 7
 1858 AD
 kaa charter adhinium:(i)bharat kaa shashan company se lekar british crown ke haathon saunpa gaya
 (ii) Ministerial posts were arranged in India
 (iii)15 sadasyon kii bharat-parishad kaa srijan hua
 (iv) Direct control of the British Parliament was established on Indian affairs
 8
 1861 AD kaa bharat shashan adhinium:governor general kii kaaryakarini parishad kaa vistaar kiya gaya,(ii)vibhageeya pranali kaa prarambh hua,(iii)governor general ko pehali baar adhyadesh jari karne kii shakti pradaan kii gai
 (iv) Governor Journal was empowered to establish the Legislative Council in Bengal, the north-western Border Province and Punjab
 9
 1892 AD kaa bharat shashan adhinium: (i)apratyaksh chunaav-pranali kii shuruyaat hui,(ii)iske dwaara rajasav evam vyay athwa bajet par bahes karne tathaa kaaryakarini se prashn poochne kii shakti di gai
 10
 1909 i0 kaa bharat shashan adhinium [marle -minto sudhaar] -(i)pehali baar muslim samudaay ke liye pruthak pratinidhitiv kaa upbandh kiya gaya
 (ii) Indians were appointed to the Executive Councils of India Secretary and Governor General
 (iii)kendriya or prantiy vidhaan-parishadon ko pehali baar bajet par vaad-vivaad karne, saarvajanik hit ke vishyon par prastaav pesh karne, poorak prashn poochne or mat dene kaa adhikaar mila
 (iv) The number of Provincial Legislative Councils was increased
 11
 Government of India Act of 1919 [montague Chelmsford Reforms] - (i) a bicameral legislature was established at the center - first the Council of States and the second Central Legislative Assembly
 rajya parishad ke sadasyon kii sankhya 60 thi; jisamen 34 nirvaachit hote the or unka kaarykaal 5 varshon kaa hota tha
 The number of members of the Central Legislative Assembly was 145, of which 104 were elected and 41 nominated
 inkaa kaarykaal 3 varshon kaa tha
 The rights of the two houses were the same
 inamen sirf ek antar tha ki bajet par sweekruti pradaan karne kaa adhikaar nichle sadan ko tha
 (ii) The system of diarchy was introduced in the provinces
 is yojana ke anusaar prantiy vishyon ko do upvargon main vibhajit kiya gaya- arakshit tathaa hastantarit
 The subjects reserved were - Finance, Landlord, Famine Assistance, Justice, Police, Pension, Criminal Castes, Raids, Newspapers, Irrigation, Waterways, Mines, Factories, Electricity, Gas, Violence, Labor Welfare, Industrial Disputes, Motor Vehicles, Small Ports and Public services etc
 hastantarit vishay -(i)shiksha, pustkaalay, sangrahalay, sthaneey swytt shashan, chikitsa sahaayta
 (ii) Department of Public Works, Excise, Industry, Weights and Measures, Control of Public Entertainment, Religious and Agrahar Donations etc
 (iii)arakshit vishay kaa prashasan governor apni kaaryakari parishad ke madhyam se karata tha; jabaki hastantarit vishay kaa prashasan prantiy vidhaan mandal ke prati uttaradaayi bhartiya mantriyon ke dwaara kiya jaataa tha
 (iv) The system of diarchy was abolished by the Act of 1935
 (v)bharat sachiv ko adhikaar diya gaya ki vah bharat main mahalekha pareekshak kii niyukti kar saktaa he
 (vi) The Act provided for the formation of a Public Service Commission in India
 12
 Government of India Act of 1935: The Act of 1935 contained 451 sections and 15 appendices
 is adhinium kii mukhya visheshtaayen is prakaar hai:(i)akhil bhartiya sangh: yah sangh 11 british praanto, 6 chif kamishnar ke kshetron or un deshi riyasaton se milakar bananaa tha, jo swechha se sangh main sammalit hon
 It was compulsory for the provinces to join the Union, but it was voluntary for the princely states
 deshi riyaasaten sangh main sammilit nahin huin or prastaavit sangh kii sthapana sambandhi ghoshnaa-patr jari karne kaa avasar hi nahin aayaa
 (ii) Provincial Autonomy: By this act, the diarchy in the provinces was abolished and provided an independent and autonomous constitutional basis
 (iii) centre main dwaidh shashan kii sthapana:kuch sangheey vishyon [suraksha, vaideshik sambandh, dharmik maamlen] ko governor general ke haathon main surakshit rakhaa gaya
 Cabinet was arranged to assist and advise the governor-general for other federal subjects, which was responsible to the Cabinet Administrator
 (iv) sangheey nyaayalay kii vyavastha:iskaa adhikaar kshetra praanton tathaa riyasaton tak vistrut tha
 a Chief Justice and two other judges were arranged in this court
 nyaayalay se sambandhit antim shakti privi council [landan] ko praapt thi
 (v) Supremacy of the British Parliament: The British Parliament had the right to make any change in this Act
 prantiy vidhaan mandal or sangheey vyavasthapika: isamen kisi prakaar kaa parivartan nahin kar sakate the
 (vi) End of Council of India: The Council of India was abolished by this Act
 (vii)sampradayik nirvachan paddati kaa vistaar: sangheey tathaa prantiy vyavasthapikaon main vibhinn sampradaayon ko pratinidhitiv dene ke liye sampradayik nirvachan paddati ko jari rakhaa gaya or uskaa vistaar angl bharatiyon - bhartiya isaayiyon, europiyanon or harijanon ke liye bhi kiya gaya
 (viii) The Act lacked preamble
 (xi)iske dwaara burma ko bharat se alag kar diya gaya, adan ko england ke aupniveshik karyaalay ke adheen kar diya gaya or baraar ko madhya praant main shaamil kar liya gaya
 13
 1947 i0 kaa bhartiya swatantraaa adhinium: british sansad main 4 july, 1947 i0 ko bhartiya swatantraaa adhinium prastaavit kiya gaya, jo 18 july, 1947 i0 ko sweekrut ho gaya
 There were 20 sections in the act
 adhinium ke pramukh praavdhaan nimna hai -(i)do adhirajyon kii sthapana: 15 agast, 1947 i0 ko bharat evam pakistan naamak do adhirajya bana die jaaengen, or unako british sarkaar satta saunp degi
 The responsibility of power will be assigned to the Constituent Assembly of both the empires
 (ii)bharat evam pakistan donon adhirajyon main ek-ek governor general honge, jinaki niyukti unke mantrimandal kii salaah se kii jaaegi
 (iii) Functioning of the Constituent Assembly as a Legislature- By the time the Constituent Assembly makes a new constitution, it will continue to function as a Legislature
 (iv)bharat-mantri ke pad samaapt kar die jaaengen
 (v) Governance by the Indian Government Act of 1935, until a new constitution is prepared by the Constituent Assembly; Till then the Indian Government Act of 1935 will rule at that time
 (vi)deshi riyasaton par britain kii sarvoparita kaa ant kar diya gaya
 They were given the freedom to join India or Pakistan in any dominion and decide their future relations

 aaie jaanate hai kab or kaise hota he grahan:surya grahan:(1)jab surya or prithvi ke bich main chandramaa aa jaataa he to surya kii chamakati sataha chandramaa ke kaaran dikhaai nahin padati he
 (2) When the sun starts to cover due to the moon, this situation is called solar eclipse
 (3)jab surya kaa ek bhaag chhip jaataa he to use aanshik suryagrahan kehete hai
 (4) When the sun is completely hidden behind the moon for some time, it is called a complete solar eclipse
 (5)purna surya grahan hameshaa amavasya ko hi hota he
 Lunar Eclipse: (1) When the Earth comes between the Sun and the Moon, the entire light of the Sun does not fall on the Moon
 ise chandragrahan kehete hai
 (2) a lunar eclipse occurs when the Sun, Earth and Moon are in a straight line
 (3)chandragrahan hameshaa poornima kii raat main hi hota he
 (4) a lunar eclipse occurs when the moon passes through the shadow of the earth maximum three times in a year
 (5)suryagrahan kii tarah hi chandragrahan bhi aanshik or purna ho saktaa he

 Team India is on a tour of the West Indies and the first Test match against the West Indies has already taken place
 donon tiimon ke bich 68 saal ke cricket rishte main kai aise record bane hai jiske bare main charchaa hoti rahati he or aage bhi hoti rahegi
 When the first Test match was played between the two teams in 1948, then in this Test match too many records were made which maintain their reputation on the pages of cricket
 is match main sar clide walcot ne jab 154 ran kii shandaar pari kheli tab unhone westeindies khilaadi ke rup main bharat ke khilaaf pehla test shatak maarane kaa record darj kiya tha
 He also had the distinction of taking the first wicket for Team India against West Indies when CR Rangachari dismissed Alan Rye of the West Indies as the first wicket
 hemchandra adhikari ne jab bharat ke liye shatak lagaaya tab ve bhi westeindies ke khilaaf shatak lagane vaale pehle bhartiya ballebaaj bane

 donon tiimon ke bich is match main or ek shandaar record bhi kaayam hua jo aaj tak nahin tut paaya
 This is the record for the most centuries in an innings
 westeindies ke chaar ballebaajon ne apni pehali pari main shatak lagaae the jo apane aap main ek record he or aaj tak donon tiimon ke bich yah record nahin tut paaya he
 Let us now come to the real issue
 jaise ham jaanate hai 60-70 ke dashak main westeindies team duniya kii sabase shandaar team maani jaati thi
 The record of how great the West Indies team was
 1961 se lekar 1967 ke bich westeindies ne alag-alag tiimon ke khilaaf lagaataar paanch test siries jiti thi
 On the foreign grounds too, the West Indies had beaten many teams, performing brilliantly
 agar bharat or westeindies ke bich hue siries kii baat kii jaae to 1948 se lekar 1971 ke bich bharat westeindies ke khilaaf ek bhi test siries nahin jeet paaya tha
 It was in 1974, Team India visited the West Indies to play a four-test series
 brijtoun main khele gayi pehle test match ko westeindies ne ek pari or 97 ran se jeeta
 The second test match was drawn
 isi tarah port of spain main jab teesraa test match shuru hua tab sab yahi soch rahe the ki tisare test main bhi westeindies kii jeet hogi
 After winning the toss, West Indies decided to bat first and scored 359 runs in their first innings
 bharat apni pehali pari main sirf 228 ran banaae
 In this way, West Indies got a lead of 131 runs from the first innings
 westeindies ne apni duusari pari 271 ran par ghoshit kar di, is tarah bharat ke saamne 403 ran kaa ek vishaal lakshya rakhaa
 The comments bharat ko itnaa bade lakshya kaa peechha karte hue match jeetna mushkil lag rahaa tha
 Before this, no team in the world could win the match chasing such a big goal
 westeindies kii team main kai shandaar gendbaaz the
 It was not easy for the Indian batsmen to face them
 lekin bharat kii kismat main kuch or likhaa hua tha
 Team India won in this match and Team India also held the record against West Indies
 is jeet ke hero the sunil gavaskar or gundappa vishwanath
 Vishwanath is the brother-in-law of Gavaskar
 jija-saale donon ne milakar westeindies ke gendbaazon kii kaaphi dhulaai kii thi
 In front of these two shorter batsmen, the long bowlers of the West Indies were seen kneeling
 salaami ballebaaj ke rup main sunil gavaskar ne 102 ran kii shandaar pari kheli, vishwanath kamaal kii ballebaaji karte hue 112 ran par note-out rahe or bharat ko jeet dilwaai
 Mahendra Amarnath also had an innings of 85 runs
 itihaas main yah pehali baar hua tha jab koi bhi team 400 se bhi zyada ran kaa lakshya kaa peechha karte hue match jiti thi
 Though later this record was definitely broken but the record between the two teams is still intact

 yah ek pari main sabase zyada shatak maarane kaa record he

 chaliye ab asli mudde par aate he

 yah 1974 kii baat he, team india ne chaar test siries khilne ke liye westeindies kaa daura kiya tha

 doosraa test match dra rahaa

 India scored just 228 runs in their first innings

 tippaniyan India found it difficult to win the match chasing such a big target

 vishwanath, gavaskar ke jija hai

 yachika main kaha gaya he ki ye act nyaaypalika kii aazaadee main khalal daalata he lihaaja ise khatm kiya janaa chahie
 Kavita is the disciple of Devi the Great Khali
 kendriya grih mantri rajnath singh ne guuruuvaar ko loksabhaa main kashmir ke mudde par bayaan dete hue kaha ki pradhanmantri puure halaat par chintit hai

 bharat main jo bhi aatanki gatividhiyaan ho rahi hai, unke peeche pakistan kaa hi haath he

 'bispi or tiemasi ne rajyasabha main mayawati ke khilaaf upi bijepi ke upaadhyaksh dayashankar ke bayaan ko lekar charchaa ke liye notice diya he
 TMC leader Derek o'brien has demanded the arrest of Dayashankar Singh
 is mudd par buudhvaar ko bhi sadan main jamkar hangaamaa hua tha

 vahiin GST jaise ahm bill par ab tak sansad main sahmati nahin ban pai he
